The disaster area is vast, covering almost the entire province with countless wounds, which is heartbreaking. The disaster has persisted in dozens of counties, which is truly the most severe in the country and unprecedented in history. Although we are urgently trying to remedy the situation, the reserves are depleted, and the people are deeply impoverished, which is not something that can be solved by small amounts. We need everyone's support. Your esteemed newspaper has the duty to uphold public opinion and promote the disaster situation in Jiangxi Province as much as possible, so that the focus of the disaster in the country will be shifted to Jiangxi, and the survivors after the catastrophe will be bathed in the warmth of spring. We are truly grateful for your kindness. We hereby send this telegram to Chen Weixi, for your information and guidance. Bao Shouyin, Hong Benli, and Xu Guozhi, Inspectors of the Jiangxi Disaster Relief Committee of the National Government.

Telegram from Wenzhou: To Shenbao and all the Money Trade Associations in major cities: Your newspaper reported that the Ministry of Finance has revised the Business Tax in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, changing the taxation of the Money Trade to 10 per mille of the capital amount, which has caused panic among the people. We recently sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance, stating: "To the esteemed Ministry of Finance: We have investigated that the current standard for classifying business taxes and collecting tax rates in Zhejiang Province stipulates that the Money Trade is taxed at 2 per mille of the capital amount, and we have heard that the Ministry has revised it to increase it to 10 per mille, which is shocking. We believe that banks and money houses both belong to financial institutions and are both industries that support commerce. Their business does not deal with goods, so there has never been a tax on them in the past. And since the banking industry has been specially exempted from business tax, the Money Trade should also be exempted by analogy. How can the Ministry fail to investigate clearly and intend to tax the Money Trade at 2 per mille of the capital amount, and the Ministry's revision is even more severe, with rumors of increasing it to 10 per mille? We are all confused and frightened. If the rumors are true, the Money Trade will suddenly increase its burden and will inevitably be weakened and decline, which will greatly affect the merchants and people. We dare not to take the liberty of sending a telegram requesting the Ministry to investigate and verify, and earnestly request that it be exempted according to the precedent of banks, so as to show fairness and security to the business community. We are extremely anxious. The Money Trade Association of Yongjia bows." This matter concerns the vital interests of the Money Trade, so we implore everyone to uphold justice. We anxiously await your response. The Money Trade Association of Yongjia bows.

Important News

Bandits in Baoduguo Are Being Encircled and Suppressed 76

General Offensive Order on April 1st

A communication from Jinan states that Han Fuqu is determined to eradicate the long-standing bandits in Baoduguo. In addition to using his own divisions to vigorously suppress them, he is also coordinating with friendly troops in Shandong to implement a large encirclement. Han himself has also gone to the front line to command. As of today (the 30th), he is still in Qufu. It is reported that the bandits in the area are divided into three groups: (1) Sun Meisong, the brother of Sun Meiyao, who robbed the train in Lincheng, has a group of about 3,000 people entrenched in the Baoduguo stronghold; (2) Yin Shigui has a group entrenched in Mengshan with about 3,000 people; (3) Wang Baichuan has the smallest group with only a few hundred people entrenched in Julingguo, which belongs to Linqu County. The 74th Division, under Qiao Lizhi, is currently encircling and suppressing the bandits with seven battalions. The bandits are stubbornly resisting on the mountain, relying on the terrain, and there are frequent fierce battles. The first gate of Julingguo has been blown up by the 74th Division's artillery. The bandits on the mountain rely entirely on the water source at the first gate for drinking water. Now that it has been blown up, the bandits are quite frightened, and some have already surrendered. The bandit area is a continuous series of mountains, and the northern part is particularly difficult to attack because of the numerous mountains and valleys. Therefore, the strength of the troops suppressing the bandits is the strongest in the Boshan area. Han Fuqu himself is serving as the commander-in-chief, with the 3rd Route Army as the main force. Gu Liangmin's 22nd Division, Lei Taiping's Pistol Brigade are responsible for Sishui, Mengyin and Fei counties, Zhan Shutang's 58th Brigade is responsible for Yishui, Cao Fulun's direct troops of the 29th Division and Qiao Lizhi's 74th Division are responsible for Linqu, and Ning Chunxiao's 64th Brigade is responsible for Boshan. Cao Fulun is responsible for commanding the northern route (Qingzhou, Linqu, Yishui, Boshan). On the side of the friendly troops, Ma Hongkui's cavalry is in Teng County, Wang Jun's 7th Division is in Lincheng, and Chen Yaohan's 26th Division is in Linyi. All the troops suppressing the bandits have reached their destinations and are carrying out reconnaissance. It is reported that a general offensive order will be issued on April 1 to jointly suppress the bandits in order to eliminate them completely.

The Qingdao Merchants' Strike Has Not Been Resolved 77

Another Petition to Party and Government Authorities

Qingdao Correspondence: The strike of Qingdao's local product merchants has lasted for more than ten days without any sign of resolution. On the 28th, at 2 PM, the merchants united and held a large-scale petition with approximately 700 representatives. Each person held a small flag and marched in formation, shouting slogans of petition along the way. They first arrived at the Municipal Party Headquarters, where four petition representatives, Liang Heping, Chen Bingjin, Zhang Yanzhan, and Shen Ziyi, met with Hou Shenglin, the Municipal Steering Committee member, and presented four requests: (1) Send another telegram to the Central Government urging approval of the merchants' demands. (2) Request the Commodity Inspection Bureau to temporarily grant exemption from inspection and fees, and also send a letter to the Jiaohai Customs to allow passage. (3) Goods shipped to Hong Kong should not be treated as foreign trade. (4) The Commodity Inspection Bureau should declare that the revenue collected from merchants should be used for the benefit of merchants. They questioned the purpose of last year's income of more than 300,000 yuan. Committee Member Hou replied that the first item could be handled accordingly, and the remaining items would be discussed and handled jointly with the Municipal Government and the Inspection Bureau. After the representatives withdrew, they reported the petition situation to the public. The entire group then went to the Municipal Government, where the representatives met with Secretary-General Hu Jiafeng to explain their intentions. Mr. Hu also promised to work with the Party Headquarters to find a proper solution. On the one hand, he would send another telegram to the Central Government; on the other hand, he would negotiate with the Inspection Bureau to request temporary exemption from inspection and fees. He also advised the public not to go to the bureau to petition, to avoid causing trouble. Subsequently, Yang Jinsheng, the Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, went to the front of the Municipal Government to persuade the public, stating that the Party and government authorities would definitely find a way to resolve the issue as soon as possible, to eliminate the merchants' suffering and achieve satisfactory results. The merchants, satisfied that the Party and government authorities had accommodated their demands, then returned in formation. When passing by the Commodity Inspection Bureau, they shouted various slogans. The Public Security Bureau, fearing an accident, had already dispatched dozens of armed police officers to the vicinity of the bureau to maintain order, so no incident occurred. The merchants also printed and distributed an open letter to all sectors, requesting unified support (the full text is omitted).

Guangdong Rice Merchants Resist Anhui Province's Rice License Tax 78

If It Is Not Abolished, They Will Purchase From Vietnam and Siam

Guangzhou Correspondence: Anhui Province's recent collection of rice license taxes has affected Guangdong Province's rice supply. The turmoil has not yet subsided. The Guangdong rice merchants have stopped purchasing Wuhu rice for many days. In February alone, the Wuhu rice merchants were forced by the Anhui government to pay rice license taxes of approximately 200,000 yuan. After the local rice merchants strongly protested, the collected rice tax was handed over to the Wuhu Chamber of Commerce for temporary preservation, pending resolution by the Central Government. However, the Anhui Provincial Government still used force to compel payment of the tax within five days, and the rice purchased by the Guangdong merchants has been detained. Therefore, the Guangdong rice merchants specially sent representative Li Mengzhuang back to Guangdong to report the turmoil and the current stalemate to the Guangdong Rice Bran Association and the Grain Association. The two rice and grain associations held a meeting on the 23rd, during which Mr. Li attended and reported on the current situation of the rice tax. He stated that when he set off to return to Guangdong, the Anhui government had given the Wuhu Chamber of Commerce five days to hand over the preserved tax money. Furthermore, Guangdong rice ships would not be allowed to leave until the case was resolved. Upon hearing the news, the colleagues of the Rice and Grain Association were indignant and immediately decided to purchase rice from places such as Vietnam and Siam instead. If the Anhui rice license tax is not abolished, Guangdong Province will never purchase Anhui rice. On the one hand, they sent another telegram to Chen Diaoyuan, the Chairman of the Anhui Provincial Government, urging him to quickly abolish the rice license tax and not impose restrictive levies. On the other hand, they telegraphed the Wuhu Chamber of Commerce to return the preserved tax money to the rice merchants or be responsible for its safekeeping and not allow powerful individuals to take it away. The two telegrams were sent out on the 24th. The original text is excerpted as follows: (1) To Chairman Chen of the Anhui Provincial Government: The collection of export license fees for rice in Anhui Province has been repeatedly ordered to be abolished by the Executive Yuan. However, the Wuhu Rice License Bureau still forcibly collects them and even prevents transportation, which is confusing. The collection of rice license fees hinders the agriculture and commerce of your province and affects the food supply of neighboring regions. Our public party and country have entrusted us with heavy responsibilities and should consider this. If there is an urgent need, it seems appropriate to seek other solutions. It should be known that rice is essential for people's livelihood. Imposing harsh levies sets a bad precedent that is difficult to eradicate and will be criticized by future generations. Yangcheng nurtured Jin and was clumsy in collecting taxes, while Duke Huan dominated Qi and even prohibited hoarding. Constitutional decrees and virtuous reputations are everlasting. We hope that you will consider this carefully and do good, benefiting not only the people of Anhui and Guangdong. We earnestly implore you and await your orders. (2) To the Guang Zhao Public Institute and the Wuhu General Chamber of Commerce: Regarding the rice license case, please persevere to the end and await resolution by the Central Government. Any payment of license fees on behalf of others will not be recognized. The tax money preserved by your association must not be taken away. Our association has telegraphed the Executive Yuan, strictly ordering a stop to the collection and approving the return of the preserved money by the Chamber of Commerce. Respectfully, Guangdong Rice Bran Industry Association and Grain Industry Association (March 25th).

Shantou Municipal Government Mediates Foreign Shipping Company's Price Increase Case 79

The Price Increase Issue Will Be Fundamentally Resolved

The Travel Association's Patrol Team Is Removed

Shantou Correspondence: The foreign shipping companies in Shantou monopolized the Singapore and Southeast Asian routes, which was resisted by all sectors. The Travel Association issued a notice to all inns and dispatched partners to form 18 patrol teams, each with 28 members, to take turns monitoring the land and sea checkpoints, prohibiting those going to Southeast Asia from boarding the ships of the foreign shipping companies. However, there were no fewer than a thousand passengers waiting in Shantou for ships to Siam, which caused great anxiety. The Shantou foreign shipping company agents then lobbied the inns to send passengers to board their ships, reducing ticket prices, providing special treatment for tea, water, meals, and dishes on board, and advising passengers to petition the Municipal Government to remove the patrol teams. On the 26th, more than 300 overseas Chinese going to Siam petitioned the Municipal Government. The organizers of the petition group were the Pu Ning Gang Inn, the Tai Feng Jieyang Gang, the Tong An Chaoyang Gang, the Mao Xing Nan Cheng Chaoan Gang, and the De Li Xing Chenghai Gang. Each invited dozens of passengers going to Siam and requested Luo Yunjie, Xu Zonghao, and Lin Guoying, the three directors of the Shantou Overseas Chinese Federation, to represent them and go to the Municipal Government to petition. The main points of their petition were: "The Travel Association, on the pretext of the foreign shipping companies increasing the price of tickets to Singapore, has jointly resisted the ships going to Siam that have not increased prices, and has dispatched armed patrols to guard the coast, causing partners to dare not send passengers and passengers to dare not disembark freely. A few days ago, Yuanli increased the ticket price to Annam by two yuan per passenger, but passengers could still board freely. Why are the Siam ships subject to unreasonable restrictions? We are forced by livelihood to go to Siam to make a living. If we are delayed for a long time and wait for the turmoil to resolve, once our travel expenses are exhausted, we will inevitably have no funds to buy tickets or be unable to pay taxes upon arrival in Siam, hindering our employment and leading to a desperate cry. We are about to exhaust our travel expenses in Shantou. In any case, we must board the Zhangjiakou and Xialishi ships on the 26th to go abroad." At that time, Mayor Zhang received the representatives and, after learning the details, immediately issued a hand decree ordering the foreign shipping companies not to increase the price of tickets to Singapore, maintaining the original price of 36 yuan per passenger. At that time, representatives of the Anti-Price Increase Committee also arrived at the Municipal Government, advocating for a further reduction of 5 jiao, while representatives of the foreign shipping companies demanded an increase of 2 yuan, i.e., 38 yuan per passenger. The dispute was only between 2 yuan and 5 jiao, which should not prolong the turmoil. Subsequently, Mayor Zhang issued another hand decree ordering the opposition committee to quickly remove the armed patrol team and not to prevent overseas Chinese from boarding ships to Siam, and ordering the Public Security Bureau to send police officers to advise the Travel Association groups that the price increase of ship tickets to Singapore was being mediated, and if the ticket prices to Siam had not increased, the sub-associations should not uniformly resist, hindering overseas Chinese from going abroad. At this point, the petition group felt satisfied and returned to their hotels. That afternoon, the Travel Association's patrol team also withdrew from the customs, and the Public Security Bureau dispatched police to patrol the streets along the coast. All slogans were also torn down, and the hotels sent the overseas Chinese to the Zhangjiakou and Xialishi ships that afternoon, which set sail for Siam that evening. However, in order to seek a complete solution, the Municipal Government convened representatives from the Anti-Price Increase Committee and the foreign shipping companies again on the morning of the 27th to find a fair solution as soon as possible (27th).

Taiyuan Dismisses Various Agencies 80

Taiyuan Correspondence: Shanxi's military reorganization is still unable to proceed due to a lack of funds for demobilization. The provincial government has recently engaged in the dismissal of political agencies. In addition to the Ordnance Factory, which has already laid off more than 2,000 employees, the provincial government decided yesterday to dismiss the Village Administration Office, Statistics Office, Tax Administration Office, Drama Improvement Association, and Political Examination Committee, as they do not comply with the central government's legal requirements. They will be taken over by the Provincial Finance Department and the Civil Affairs Department. The Financial Restructuring Office, the Party and Government Academy, the Model Propaganda Institute, and the Shanxi Political Report will be scaled down and temporarily retained. After the implementation of this decision, the number of unemployed officials in Taiyuan will increase considerably.

In recent days, the sharp decline in provincial currency has affected the people's livelihood, causing extreme panic. As a result, rumors have spread, and the people's hearts are uneasy. Fearing that unscrupulous individuals will disrupt local security, the authorities have increased the number of joint military and police investigation teams in addition to the existing garrison troops to carry out defense. Therefore, Taiyuan remains relatively peaceful. Regarding the request of teachers and staff from various schools for salary payments, the association issued a declaration yesterday, stating that if the authorities fail to understand, they will have no choice but to resign collectively and seek other means of livelihood. Judging from the current situation, it is feared that a teaching strike will eventually occur, which is also a problem of great concern in Taiyuan (March 28th).

Shanxi Provincial Antiquities Exhibition 81

Exhibiting Antiquities From 5,000 Years Ago

Unique Types, Approximately Tens of Thousands

Taiyuan Correspondence: Shanxi archaeologists Wei Juxian and others excavated many antiquities last year at the Han Fenyin Houtu Temple in Wanquan County, southern Shanxi. Now, Mr. Wei and others, for the convenience of the public, have organized and cataloged the various items and opened an antiquities exhibition at the Confucius Temple Library. The exhibition began on the 27th, and many people came to visit. The exhibition has various explanatory signs and photographs posted on the walls, and Wei Juxian himself is present to guide visitors. The antiquities occupy two rooms, inner and outer. The items displayed in the outer room were excavated from the Jingcun Waza slope in Wanquan County and are all coarse and fine pottery from 5,000 years ago, such as jars, bottles, pots, women's earrings, hairpins, and bone tools. The items displayed in the inner room were collected from Xidu Village and Yanziyi Pagoda near the Han Fenyin Houtu Temple in Wanquan County. Most of them are coarse and fine pottery from 2,000 years ago, with bricks and tiles being the most numerous. The large tiles are about two or three feet long and one or two feet wide, painted with Bagua (eight trigrams), Taiji (yin-yang symbol), and other patterns. The clay is solid, the patterns are exquisite, and the names are numerous, which are rare in the world. There are approximately tens of thousands of objects, large and small. Among them, the most peculiar is a male reproductive organ made of pottery, about two or three inches long, with the glans and urethra as lifelike as the real thing. According to its label, ancient people worshiped male reproductive organs the most, so they made this object from pottery and displayed it in their homes as an ornament. As for the Han Fenyin Houtu Temple, it was built in the fourth year of Emperor Wu of the Han Dynasty (Yuanding). At that time, many members of the imperial family lived there, so the actual noble items were exceptionally numerous. Later, the Han Dynasty declined, and most of the items were buried underground. The items excavated today are probably of this kind (March 27th).

Zou Shangyou Is Internally Appointed as Secretary-General

Japanese in Yanbian Consolidate Their Defense 83

Based on Unequal Treaties

The Conspiracy of Aggression Is Increasingly Exposed

World Society Shenyang Correspondence: The Japanese are carrying out various conspiracies to invade the Northeast in all aspects, including diplomacy, military affairs, and industry. There are countless undisclosed plans. Recently, they have become even more aggressive. Their military plan in the border area has been detected by our Yanbian authorities. The Japanese have always regarded the so-called Jiandao as their sphere of influence in that area, meaning it is located between China and Korea. According to the maps made by the Japanese, Jiandao includes the Yanbian area, such as Longjing Village, Juzi Street, Toudaogou, Baicaogou, and the plains north of the Tumen River. The Japanese manage this area based on the so-called Jiandao Agreement signed on September 4, 1909. According to the content of the agreement, there are five articles: (1) The Tumen River is the border. (2) Open Longjing Village, Juzi Street, Toudaogou, and Baicaogou as commercial ports. (3) Korean farmers should be allowed to live north of the Tumen River. (4) Japanese people have the freedom to do business and reside in the mixed-residence area north of the Tumen River. (5) Extend the Jichang Railway to connect with the Huining Railway in Korea. The Japanese use this unequal treaty to manage Yanbian, and their influence has now far exceeded the scope of the treaty. The so-called Jiandao has become a Japanese colony in an invisible way. The Japanese have established a police agency to govern the people of Yanbian, treating our country's sovereignty as nothing for a long time. In the past one or two years, the movement of the people of the Northeast to recover national sovereignty has been rising. Various anti-Japanese groups have been established in the Jiandao area. Our country's military police also hate the Japanese invasion, and there have been repeated conflicts with the unreasonable Japanese police. The killing of Japanese police in Jilin last year was one example. In view of this, the Japanese very much want to send troops to

Page 8

garrison the area. However, this action is related to international relations and they do not dare to openly carry it out. Therefore, they have increased their defense on the border in order to take advantage of opportunities. The total number of Japanese police stationed along the approximately 200-mile-long border line from the Yalu River to the Tumen River has reached 12,700, with the establishment of gun emplacements, observation towers, airfields, and wireless and wired telegraph stations. There are also shallow-water destroyers patrolling the Tumen and Yalu Rivers. Even on the opposite bank, which is under the jurisdiction of our country's sovereignty, the Japanese police openly have resident offices. Our side endures and retreats, and does not dare to establish police agencies along the riverbanks to avoid conflicts, which has caused the Japanese arrogance to intensify and act recklessly. It is truly lamentable.

Wu Tiecheng's Speech on the Northeast Under Japanese and Russian Aggression 85

Shenyang Correspondence: The Liaoning National Diplomacy Association recently held a banquet for Wu Tiecheng, a member of the Central Committee, and his staff at the Fanyang Youth Association, and invited Mr. Wu to give a speech. Mr. Wu spoke on "The Northeast Under Japanese and Russian Aggression." The following is a record of his speech:

"Chairman, comrades, today I am honored to receive such a warm reception from the Liaoning National Diplomacy Association. I, on behalf of my colleagues, express my deep gratitude. I have been to the Northeast several times. Every time I go to the Northeast and come into contact with it, the Northeast gives me a better impression, more understanding, and deeper understanding. This impression, understanding, and understanding not only make me feel a closer relationship with the Northeast, but also often make me more patriotic, especially the kind of concern and attachment to the Northeast. Why? Because the Northeast is the most important gateway to northern China, and it goes without saying that the products are abundant. Just taking the international relations alone, the Northeast also occupies a very important position. Since the Northeast stands in such an important position, it is naturally and naturally particularly closely related to China's national defense and economic survival. Simply put, everything that happens in the Northeast often involves the safety of the entire China and makes people not forget to care about the Northeast, feeling that the Northeast has a close relationship with themselves. Therefore, when I came to the Northeast to comfort the army on the order of the Central Government last time, I issued two slogans after returning from Jihai: "I don't know how great China is until I go to the Northeast, and I don't know how dangerous China is until I go to the Northeast." This is because of this reason. However, there are some people who are insensitive. They have always only known one end of the pros and cons and do not know the other end of the pros and cons. They can only see the economic oppression of the imperialist initiators and cannot see the various oppressions of the imperialists other than the economy. This problem is especially serious among the people in Guannei because they can only see the imperialists bringing various things to exchange for our money every day, and they don't feel any personal relationship with the rest. But the Northeast is very different. In addition to money, there are also political oppression, military oppression, and various other most profound and humiliating oppressions all gathered in the Northeast. It can be said that this is the most severely oppressed place. Therefore, the people of the Northeast feel the pain of the imperialists' aggression particularly deeply, and their patriotic enthusiasm is far more ardent than that of the people in Guannei. Every morning I wake up, open the window, and look out, I feel my spirit excited, also because I feel that the claws of the imperialists are all unfolded in front of me. Therefore, the people in Guannei, no matter how negligent they are of the imperialists' aggression, will immediately feel the personal interests of the people in the Northeast outside Guannei. Under this kind of restraint, under this kind of oppression, it is a natural result that no matter what kind of person feels excited. From this point of view, it can also be seen that the patriotism of the people outside Guannei is more enthusiastic than that of the people in Guannei. What's more, the people in Guannei already know that they are about to reach the point of direct contact with the imperialists. We can imagine by looking at the establishment of the Liaoning National Diplomacy Association. Just now I heard the chairman say that the establishment of the Liaoning National Diplomacy Association was initiated when the people of Liaoning with lofty ideals felt the urgency of foreign aggression during the last Red Russian disturbance in order to make the people of the whole country pay attention to the issue of the Northeast. In other words, it was established in accordance with the Prime Minister's instructions that in order to seek freedom and equality for China, we must awaken the people. Therefore, the greatest proposition of the National Diplomacy Association is to seek freedom and equality for China, that is, to make the whole country pay attention to the aggression of the red and white imperialists in the Northeast and to seek freedom and equality for China. I often see in the newspapers that your association has done a lot of extremely consistent work, which makes me very admire and agree. Unfortunately, I have never had much material on international diplomacy to contribute to you, and some of them cannot be announced frankly, which is a great regret. Now, regarding the aggression of the red and white imperialists, I will briefly announce some of what I know, which can also be used as a reference for your association.

The Northeast has vast land and abundant products. Therefore, when the current great powers' population problem and capitalism have already reached a state of saturation, there is not an imperialist who does not want to open a new road to the Northeast and benefit from the Northeast, just like the former four-country loan group also wanted to enter the Northeast to share the benefits. However, at that time, Japan, for its own vital interests, joined forces with Russia to suppress the four-country loan group, and in the end, the four-country loan group stopped from then on. Now, the southern part of the Northeast is oppressed by white Japanese imperialism, and the northern part is invaded by red Soviet Russian imperialism. And the sinister policies of these two imperialists had already been arranged by the Russian Foreign Minister Sakonov and Japanese Katsura Taro in the era of the Russian emperor through a secret agreement to divide the so-called Manchuria and Mongolia. Later, after the October Revolution in Russia, although it announced the natural abandonment of all unequal treaties, it still traditionally inherited the aggressive policies of the imperial era towards the invasion of Manchuria and Mongolia and has not changed its attitude in the slightest until now, just like the incident on the Chinese Eastern Railway. Not only did they not fulfill the treaty, but in the end they had to use force to oppress China. They also disregarded Article 5 of the outline signed in May of the thirteenth year and still controlled Outer Mongolia. Are these things the attitude that a so-called revolutionary socialist country should have? In fact, there is not a single difference from the imperialist capitalist countries. Not only are they using the Chinese Eastern Railway as a base for propaganda and redification, but in order to invade the Northeast, they are also trying their best to buy off bandits and hooligans in China to disrupt China's public security and destroy China's peace, so that the areas such as Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi, which have always been known for their richness, have been messed up. This shows the sinister intentions of Red Russia. The reason why China cannot start construction now is because the bandits and hooligans, reactionaries, and so-called communists bought by Red Russia have disrupted China's public security and made the people of China uneasy (To be continued)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 86

The Public Security Bureau Strictly Prohibits Officials From Corruption. Shen Jing, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, has always been strict in investigating and handling tobacco and gambling cases, fearing that there would be impersonators of public security personnel cheating and extorting money outside, or that unscrupulous officials would be corrupt and harbor them. Therefore, a notice was issued stating that no matter who it is, if they encounter the above situation and have evidence to point to, they will be given a heavy reward once they are reported. However, they must not report out of personal grudges, otherwise they will be punished in return.

Scheduled Election of National Assembly Representatives. After the National Assembly representative election, the county's national register was submitted to the province. The order was issued that the Sihong Town Chamber of Commerce had complete procedures and met the election qualifications. The members of the association had the right to vote. The ballots, ballot boxes, and the general list of candidates were collected. The county government's preparation work has been completed. The election will be held on the 3rd of this month. The county election supervisor, Jin Qingzhang, will go to Sihong on the 2nd to monitor the election to show solemnity.

Territory Controlled by the Sanqing Township Team. The bandit suppression command of the four counties of Songjiang, Jinshan, Shanping, and Pinghu convened a Sanqing conference in the four counties the other day and decided to implement the Qingcha on schedule. Each area with bandits was assigned a Qingcha team to assist the local government in handling it. A total of three Qingxiang teams were organized in three districts. Its regional control is based on the fourth district (Ganxiang), fifth district (Lvxu), sixth district (Zhangyan), seventh district (Langxia), and eighth district (Jinshanwei) of Jinshan; the twelfth district (Tinglin), fifteenth district (Caoxu), and sixteenth district (Shanyang) of Songjiang; and the second district (Zhapu), third district (Xinkua), and fourth district (Xincang) of Pinghu, each stationed a team responsible for the Qingcha.

Suzhou 87

Regarding the Announcement of Prison Guards for the Reformatory: The Higher Court's recruitment examination for reformatory prison guards was announced yesterday (the 1st). The following were selected: Chen Songhe, Hu Maoxian, He Qiu, Xia Shijun, Wang Wenzhou, Qu Rong, Zhang Zongze, Ding Lisheng, Zhong Wenfu, Ruan Yingjie, Pan Shiyao, Pu Lizhi, Xu Yuru, Jin Ximin, Sun Zaixing, Li Zhicheng, Gu Zengqing, Yang Jingqi, Xia Jintang, Tian Yufeng, Shuai Jiangong, Fei Zihua, Fang Yi, Zhi Zhen, Zhang Yizhen, Zheng Yanliang, Fan Guangyuan, Wu Zhizhen, and 28 others. They are to be dispatched immediately to the new prisons for training.

Four Kidnappers Escorted to Wujiang: The Third District of the Water Police, according to the Fourteenth Squad of Wujiang, recently escorted four kidnappers—Liang Ying'an, Li Guozhi, Pan A'kui, and He A'lian—to the area. District Chief Shen interrogated them and submitted a report to the Civil Affairs Department for review. Yesterday (the 1st), the Civil Affairs Department ordered that the kidnappers be sent to the Wujiang County Government for handling. District Chief Shen obeyed the order and instructed officers to escort Liang and the other three kidnappers to Wujiang County for disposition.

A Kidnapping Case Occurred in Chefang Town: Zhao Hongzhang, head of Zhao Family Village, near Yinguo outside Fengmen Gate, and tax collector Zhao Yongzhi, were kidnapped by bandits on March 20. Yesterday (the 1st), a letter from the bandits to Zhao Jue, the head of the household, demanded a ransom of 100,000 yuan in cash and a box cannon. Zhao Yongzhi's ransom was 60,000 yuan, plus one dozen packs of cigarettes and foreign socks. The bandits stated that the ransom must be paid within a week at Sanshan in Taihu Lake; otherwise, they would tear up the tickets. After receiving the letter, Zhao's family reported to the authorities and requested assistance in the rescue.

Wuxi 88

Major Fire on Tonghui Road: More than thirty grass sheds located between Tonghui Road and Tongqin Road, behind the First Stage, mainly inhabited by Jianghuai merchants, were destroyed by fire. Fan Jinbiao, a night watchman, resided in shed number thirteen. Around 5:30 PM the night before, a fire broke out suddenly and unexpectedly. Due to strong winds and dry weather, the fire spread rapidly. In less than half an hour, more than thirty grass sheds were completely burned down, also affecting the Xixingli Xincheng Xu sand factory workshop to the left, the Shuntaixing iron shop outside Tongqin Road. Furthermore, sixteen workshops rented by Xixing Company in Xixingli were also damaged in the front. Fortunately, Xiangtai Company had fire insurance. Other households also suffered significant losses. During the fire, a Jiangxi man named Huang Youcai seized the opportunity to steal a cotton quilt but was discovered. He was handed over to the police of the Sixth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, and three papers with symbols were found on him. His confession was vague, and he has been sent to the General Bureau for interrogation.

Provincial Order Approves Exemption from Donation for Self-Organized Feasts: After the levy of the Wuxi feast education donation began, restaurants collected the donation on behalf of the government and were able to report and remit the funds accurately. However, chefs hired for private events were affected and refused to acknowledge the donation, which affected tax revenue and hindered the business of restaurants. Restaurants petitioned for relief one after another. The county government's finance bureau jointly reported to the provincial government for instructions. Yesterday, the provincial government issued a directive stating that henceforth, households holding weddings, funerals, or celebratory events, who can clearly prove that they have a resident chef and organize the feast themselves, are permitted to be exempt from the donation. If hiring a chef, regardless of the size of the feast or whether purchasing ingredients themselves or contracting the chef, the chef should be responsible for collecting the donation in accordance with regulations to prevent evasion and maintain business operations. Director Zhuang of the Finance Bureau will separately communicate the directive for compliance.

Xu Xingzhen Commits Suicide to Follow Her Husband in Death: On February 14, the "Xiban Heng" small steamboat, owned by the Taili Company of Wuxi, sank in Nantang, drowning passenger Wang Yongxi and more than ten others. Details have been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that the deceased passenger Wang Yongxi worked at the Shanghai Commercial Press. On January 23, he married Xu Xingzhen from the Guwang Bridge Xu family in Taibo City. Xingzhen was twenty years old. After their marriage, their love was profound. Unfortunately, her husband, Wang Yongxi, tragically died. Xingzhen was overwhelmed with grief. Her in-laws repeatedly comforted her, but Xingzhen remained depressed and contemplated suicide. On the night of the 30th, she secretly swallowed raw opium in an attempt to end her life. Her family discovered her and rushed her by boat to the city and admitted her to Puren Hospital for treatment. Dr. Li Kele administered injections and provided treatment, but because she had ingested too much poison, she died around 11:00 AM the day before. Her family transported her body back to her hometown to prepare a coffin and burial. It can be called tragic.

Changzhou 89

A Robbery with Injuries Occurred in Fanghuancheng Bridge: On the night of the 30th, at around 10:00 PM, eight or nine armed robbers suddenly came to the home of Jiang Chanjin, a villager in Fanghuancheng Bridge, located in the fifth district of Wujin, southeast of Jiaoxi Town. They restrained Jiang Chanjin and demanded silver dollars, resulting in him being beaten and severely injured. After looting, the robbers fled, taking with them an estimated loss of 150 yuan in silver dollars, as well as clothing. The local public security station has dispatched police to investigate.

Bandit Song Yaoda Captured in Qishuyan: The First Squad of the Tenth Water Police Team stationed in Qishuyan, Wujin, recently received a tip that bandit Song Yaoda was hiding in Baizhang Town and was involved in a robbery case. The squad immediately dispatched officers to Baizhang on the 31st and apprehended him. He was taken to the city on the 1st for interrogation. Salt Prices Increased: Wujin Salt Public Depot was ordered to increase salt prices starting April 1, with each dan (unit of weight) increasing by 3 jiao (one-tenth of a yuan) and each jin (unit of weight) by 3 li (one-thousandth of a yuan). The additional revenue is specifically designated to subsidize the repayment of foreign debts. The Depot has informed all salt merchants, and starting today (the 1st), the original price of 320 wen (unit of currency) per jin has been changed to 330 wen per jin.

Impersonating a Soldier and Violating the Law - Execution by Firing Squad: The Third Regiment of the Changzhou Garrison recently apprehended a man named Zhou Jie (23 years old, from Liuyang, Hunan) for impersonating a soldier. It was discovered that he was selling opium and using counterfeit money. After interrogation, he confessed. The Capital Garrison Headquarters approved his execution by firing squad. On the afternoon of the 31st, Regiment Adjutant Mu Zongxi escorted Zhou Jie to Fengweidun execution ground for execution by firing squad after confirming his identity.

Jiangyin 90

Farmers in Tongzheng Township Robbed: On the afternoon of the 28th, around 9:00 PM, farmers Zhou Dougen and Zhou Jinbiao, among others in Xiazhixiang, Tongzheng Township, Zhouzhuang, were robbed by more than ten bandits, who made off with dozens of silver dollars. Before leaving, they threatened to return for a large sum of money within three days, or else they would take adverse actions.

Unidentified Male Corpse Found in Shizhuang: An unidentified male corpse was found in Shizhuang Town, Sixth District, the day before yesterday. The district office reported it to the county. Yesterday (the 31st), County Committee Public Security Bureau Chief Yin Geng, together with Coroner Cao, went to the village to examine the body. The corpse had already decomposed, and the face was blurred. There was a hemp rope beside the corpse. The injuries were difficult to identify. The town chief arranged for the corpse to be collected.

Zhenjiang 91

Qingxiang Bureau Explains Difficulties in Various Aspects: Long Tiyao, inspector of the Jiangsu Provincial Qingxiang General Bureau, discovered the following three difficulties during his inspection in Zhenjiang: (A) Regarding the investigation of household registration, the investigation of vagrants is very important, but the standard for vagrants is actually difficult to determine, and there is great difficulty during the investigation. (B) Regarding the joint guarantee and pledge, (1) if a person has committed theft in the past, but there is no improper behavior now, he should not be investigated for his past according to the law, but the neighbors on the left and right are unwilling to guarantee him because of this relationship, how should it be handled? (2) if someone has just moved in from another place and has no relatives or friends and lives in a thatched hut (most of these people work hard), and no one dares to guarantee him, what should be done? (C) Regarding defense and suppression, if the general corps members are injured or killed while suppressing bandits, there are no fixed compensation or medical expenses. If this continues, no one will dare to continue their efforts. The General Bureau should set a specific method for compensation. The above difficulties were reported to the General Bureau for instructions. Because it was important, the General Bureau immediately clarified and notified all counties to comply. The original text of the explanation is recorded below: (A) A vagrant should be someone who has no occupation, no family, and no fixed residence. (B) 1. If there are such people in any township, the township chief should inspect them at any time, and the neighbors should report their behavior to the township chief for investigation. 2. They should be ordered to find two or more people to guarantee them, otherwise they will not be allowed to build a house to live in. (C) Before the regulations on commendation and compensation by the Department of Civil Affairs are formulated and implemented, the counties should consider the budget for the security corps and handle it accordingly.

Chamber of Commerce Discusses Business Tax Issues Again: The Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce believes that the issue of the business tax rate in Jiangsu Province and the issue of each county's chamber of commerce contracting to collect the tax is of great importance. In addition to sending letters to each county's chamber of commerce, inviting representatives to come to Zhenjiang today (the 1st) to hold a meeting to discuss it together, it also convened the third temporary meeting yesterday morning at 10:00 AM to discuss the opinions on the revised business tax rate and contracting to collect the tax. The following resolutions were passed: (1) The seven principles agreed upon by the representatives of each county in Zhenjiang last time, except for the second and third items, the Chamber of Commerce should still ask each representative to continue to strive for the first, fourth, fifth, sixth, and seventh items. (2) The two principles that the collection period in the inland should not be earlier than Shanghai and the tax rate should not be higher than Shanghai should be given special attention by each representative. (3) The Chamber of Commerce believes that contracting to collect the tax is actually difficult to implement, and the Department of Finance should send personnel to collect the tax itself.

Chief of the Fifth Public Security Bureau Dismissed: The General Bureau discovered that Ma Yuebo, chief of the Fifth Public Security Bureau, was extorting illegal fees from the Tianchan Stage. The General Bureau sent inspectors to wait and watch in the area and obtained conclusive evidence. In addition to dismissing the messenger and sending him back to the bureau for interrogation, the chief of the bureau was dismissed to show a warning, as he was extorting illegal fees. In addition, Liu Kebi, the captain of the bicycle team of the bureau, led the police to Paiwan to inspect and extorted money from the villagers under the pretext of being on duty. The General Bureau also discovered this, detained him, and brought him to the bureau. Because the case was serious, in addition to dismissing him, the captain and four subordinates were sent to the court for handling according to law.

Director-General Liang Assists Local Road Construction and River Dredging: Liang Guanying, the general director of the 25th Route, gathered troops stationed in Nantong at the Nantong Club on the 31st to give a speech and examine the soldiers' various subjects. Former Construction Bureau Director Embezzled Funds - Investigation Completed: The case of the former Construction Bureau Director Yao Pengnian's embezzlement and his flight out of fear of punishment has been investigated by the province. The county committee found that Yao had embezzled more than 6,300 yuan in relief funds. The results of the investigation have been reported to the provincial government for review.

Expediting Spring Relief in the County: The spring famine situation in Tongyi is very serious. On the 31st, representatives from all walks of life met and decided to raise 15,000 yuan from industry, commerce, agriculture, and wealthy people to expedite emergency relief throughout the county. At the same time, a request was submitted to the province for the allocation of relief funds.

Reorganization of the Property Management Office: Xu Gengqi, director of the Nantong Public Funds and Property Management Office, and Bao Yun, Sun Kongyi, and Nongyin resigned due to the expiration of their terms. The county reorganized the office, but the newly appointed Zhang Shuyuan, Xu Guanxun, and Liu Shuhuang firmly refused to take office. On the 31st, the county government requested the original directors to continue their duties to avoid a prolonged stagnation of local finances. The solution to the problem remains to be seen.

Pukou 93

Jinpu Railway Bureau Increases Office Hours: Since the reorganization of the management committee of the Jinpu Railway Bureau, the members have been earnestly organizing and often stay late into the night. As a result, the work of the affiliated offices has become tense. Because most of the bureau's staff resides in Xiaguan, it has been the custom to leave the office at 5:00 PM to cross the river. The committee has now decided to increase the office hours. Starting April 1, the closing time will be extended to 6:00 PM.

Huzhou 95

Robbery Case at Luodai Bridge: The home of Shen Minxiang in Luodai Bridge, located about three li from Mayaozhen in the Nanxun District of Huzhou, was suddenly attacked by more than ten bandits armed with knives, guns, sticks, and batons at midnight on the 27th of this month. Speaking in mixed dialects, they broke down the door and entered. Four bandits restrained and beat Minxiang and his mother, while the other bandits entered and ransacked the house, stealing all clothing and other items. The total loss was about 200 yuan.

Water Police Informant Shot and Killed: A man named Tan from Henan, over 50 years old, who worked as an informant for the water police team, was suddenly shot and killed in front of his home in Jinjiaba, near Qianjin Town in the Linghu District of Huzhou, after dinner on the 25th of this month. Neighbors and family members who heard the sound came out and saw that Tan was lying dead on the ground. The murderer had fled without a trace. It is said that the reason for his murder seems to be related to the investigation of bandits.

Ningbo 96

The Hu Grandparents Were Kidnapped at the Same Time: The family of Hu Antao, a resident of Zhujiayuan, Wushan, Yuyao, has a well-to-do family and was coveted by bandits. On the evening of the 26th of this month, at around 11:00 PM, more than twenty bandits suddenly arrived. Because the Hu family's gate was unusually strong, a bandit first used a bamboo pole to climb over the wall, open the gate, and swarm in. They ransacked the house for an hour. Before leaving, they kidnapped Hu himself and his nine-year-old grandson Pu Cheng. Afterwards, the family urgently reported to the local public security bureau, which dispatched police to pursue, but the bandits had already escaped without a trace. They are currently requesting the county government to find a way to rescue the hostages.

Security Corps Member Accidentally Injures Someone with a Gun: At Zhao Zhangyan Ferry, between Lin and Lishi in the south of Yin, on the afternoon of the 28th, at 4:00 PM, Feng, a member of the security corps, Lin Haixian and Yu Bingding, accidentally injured Fang, the wife of Wu Jinsheng, in the breast and Wu Cuie, her daughter, in the head while playing with firearms. The injuries were quite serious. After someone reported it, Zhu Guang, the patrol officer of the Shishi substation, rushed to the scene with the police, investigated the incident, and ordered the injured to be immediately sent to the Central Hospital in front of the County School in this city for treatment. At the same time, he pursued the perpetrators. Wang Shanghui, the leader of the corps, captured Lin Haixian, while Yu Bingding had already fled. Lin was sent to the Yin County Public Security Bureau and then to the Yin County Local Court for interrogation.

Hefei 97

Division Executes Four Robbers by Firing Squad: Five suspected robbers - Sang Jingwen, He Kaizhi, Wang Xueyao, Qian Hongchuan, and Xia Guoqiu - who had committed more than ten robberies in the city were arrested by the detective team. He Kaizhi admitted to being a bandit and had already been executed by firing squad, but the others were evasive and refused to confess. After being taken back to the military court of the 46th Division for strict interrogation, Sang and the others confessed. Today (the 25th) at noon, the military court brought out Sang and the other four, tied them up, paraded them through the streets, and then took them to the Cai Datang execution ground and executed them by firing squad.

Letters

Letter from Rhode & Co. 98

To the Editor:

Dear Sir,

We are writing in reference to the news item in your March 30 Ningbo dispatch concerning the rebuilding of the two bridges in Ningbo. It stated that our company's engineer, Mr. Ansber, along with a prominent Shanghai businessman, inspected the two bridges in Ningbo, and suggested that the new Jiang Bridge should be moved to Lujia Daotou and the old Jiang Bridge should be moved to Dahuantou, and that the new bridge should be an automatic swivel bridge, and the construction cost of the two bridges would be about one million yuan. This is slightly inaccurate. Our company's Mr. Ansber was only commissioned to make a preliminary inspection of the existing bridge bodies and the river surface. He did not make any statements about the location of the new bridge, the style of the new bridge, or the cost. Your newspaper's Ningbo dispatch was the result of a misunderstanding. Our company is afraid that the rumors will be inaccurate and cause misunderstandings. We are writing this letter to correct the record and request that it be published in your newspaper's letter column. Thank you very much.

Sincerely,

Rhode & Co.

Swiss Merchant

March 31

Important Educational News

Ministry of Education Formulates Middle School Education Outline 99

｜Starting from the 20th Academic Year｜

County Middle Schools to be Converted into Vocational Schools or Rural Teacher Training Schools

Nanjing, 1st - The Ministry of Education has formulated an outline for middle school education in each province and city and has ordered the education departments and bureaus of each province and city to comply with it. The content stipulates that starting from the 20th academic year, county middle schools should be gradually reorganized into vocational schools or rural teacher training schools. If they cannot be reorganized, the education departments should consider the situation and order the establishment of vocational and rural teacher training courses in ordinary middle schools.

Yanjing University Law Department Specially Approved for Establishment 100

The Ministry of Education instructed the Beijing Municipal Bureau of Education: "It is hereby noted that the private law and political schools in Beijing that have been registered should submit an application to the Judicial Yuan for special approval. This has been ordered to the Bureau for compliance. Subsequently, the Board of Trustees of the Private Yanjing University submitted various documents for the Law Department of the University's Law School, requesting that they be forwarded to the Judicial Yuan for review, etc. The Ministry previously sent a letter to the Judicial Yuan, stating that the University had submitted a document for the reorganization of the Law School, including proof of registration, a draft curriculum, a list of teachers' qualifications, and a plan for facilities, requesting that it be forwarded for review and special approval. The University was approved for registration in June of the 18th year by the Ministry and in December of the 19th year, it was reported that the Applied Social Sciences Institute would be reorganized into the Law School and that a Law Department would be added. This was also ordered to be approved. The original documents are sent with this letter requesting review. The Judicial Yuan replied that the University's Law School's multi-year curriculum and various facilities are quite complete and should be specially approved for establishment. In accordance with Article 4 of the Judicial Yuan's Regulations for Special Approval of Private Law and Political Schools, it is hereby consulted with the Examination Yuan for filing and sent to the government for publication. The same will be conveyed to the Bureau."

Hu Clan's Charitable Estate's Donation for Education is Commendable 101

The Ministry of Education commended Hu Clan's Charitable Estate for donating funds to establish schools in Tianshang Village, Wuxi.

The Ministry of Education issued a special instruction to the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education: "All documents have been received. The Hu Clan's Charitable Estate is enthusiastic about education and has generously donated houses, land, and cash totaling 180,000 yuan. It has been verified that this is true and a Class A certificate of merit should be awarded in accordance with the regulations on commendation for donating funds to establish schools. The Ministry will specially submit a request to the Executive Yuan to be forwarded to the National Government for a clear order of commendation to inspire encouragement. In addition to the special submission, a Class A certificate of merit is hereby issued to be forwarded."

Ji Da Issues Notice to Overseas Chinese Students Returning Home for Attention 103

The Nanyang-Americas Culture Department of Ji Da recently issued a notice to overseas Chinese, directing Nanyang-America各报馆各商会各书报社各公共圑体 to forward information to students and parents returning home to study. The notice states that the school was founded in Nanjing and moved to Shanghai. Over the past 20 years, it has spared no effort in planning and implementing overseas Chinese education. As a result, more and more overseas Chinese students are coming to study. The department is affiliated with the school and is responsible for communicating with overseas Chinese. In view of this situation, we are all very happy. However, many students overseas are not familiar with the situation in the interior, so they arrive at different times, making it very inconvenient for students to study abroad. Therefore, we will briefly outline the new regulations of the Ministry of Education and the school's enrollment regulations as a general guide for those returning to study. In recent years, the Ministry of Education has been working hard to rectify public schools, and has set fixed regulations for holidays and exam periods. It has also unified the enrollment process, with one exam held every year during the summer vacation, except for special circumstances. Since our school is a national school, it cannot be an exception. Our department has been reporting to overseas elders about overseas communication for many years. However, many overseas students are too eager to go to school and do not have time to consider the exam period. Not only do they come to the school during the annual holidays to request admission, but the timing of their return is also inconsistent. It is very inconvenient to refuse them, as it is a pity to deny them the opportunity to study. However, accepting them would disrupt the regulations. After repeated consideration, we deeply feel that the previous accommodating measures were originally a temporary expedient. If they continue to be extended, they will greatly hinder the school's administration and facilities. Therefore, the recent school affairs meeting has repeatedly stated that new students will be admitted in accordance with the school's regulations. June 24 is the registration date, and July 6-8 is the exam date. Applications will be rejected before the exam date and no exceptions will be made after the exam date. We hope that students returning from overseas to study will make preparations early and arrive in Shanghai before July 1 to register and take the exam on time to avoid difficulties. We hereby announce this and wish you all the best.

Central Film and Cultural Propaganda Committee (Continued) 104

(II) Promoting the Doctrine of People's Rights: For four thousand years, the Chinese people, ruled by the tyranny of the imperial system, have devoted their lives to serving the emperor and lack understanding of the rights and obligations that citizens should enjoy. Fortunately, thanks to the clarion call of the late Premier Sun, the people were awakened and knew that the world belonged to the people and was not the private property of one family or individual. However, the hidden power of warlords and local tyrants has not been eliminated, and the people still lack understanding of the doctrine of people's rights under repeated oppression. This is all due to a lack of propaganda. The only plan for now is to make films that compare the disadvantages of the people's abandonment of their rights with the benefits of people in other countries using their rights to imply the difference. First, let the people know, and then they can act. There has never been a case of someone knowing they have rights but not wanting to enjoy them. The problem is that they do not know.

(III) Promoting Nationalism: A nation has its own special status, and a nation has its own special culture. Therefore, land, people, and culture are the three major elements of nation-building. Our country's land is shrinking, the people are declining, and the culture is collapsing. The country will cease to be a country. How can we continue to fail to improve ourselves? The lessons of the past, such as India's resistance to Britain, Korea's resistance to Japan, and Morocco and Annam's resistance to France, are all deeply affected by the brutal rule of other nations. All those with blood and qi are heartbroken and resentful. Therefore, there is this final struggle for the people. Moreover, our nation has long been under the invasion of various imperialisms and is in imminent danger. If we still do not vigorously promote nationalism to give the general public a considerable nationalistic ideology, then in the future, when the government faces a diplomatic emergency, the people will be driven by nationalism in their hearts and will unite into a strong and powerful rear. Its power should not be ignored. However, this kind of effect can only be achieved through film propaganda. (To be continued)

Municipal Education Bureau Orders Elementary Schools to Apply for Registration Again 105

At the Latest, by the End of the Summer Vacation This Year

｜Otherwise, Ordered to Stop Enrollment or Forced to Close

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau yesterday issued instructions to private elementary schools that have not been registered: "It is hereby noted that all private schools at all levels in this city should organize a board of directors in accordance with the regulations on private schools and apply for registration in sequence. The Bureau has repeatedly ordered compliance within a limited time. It is now found that there are many private elementary schools in this city that have not yet applied for registration. According to the regulations of the Ministry, the deadline for registration is at the latest the end of the summer vacation this year, which is the day before the start of the 20th academic year. Those who fail to register after the deadline will be ordered to stop enrollment or forced to close. The deadline is approaching, and the Bureau will handle it in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry and will no longer be lenient. In addition to separate orders, it is hereby urgently ordered that all unregistered elementary schools in this city comply and apply for registration before the deadline. Do not hesitate any longer. This is an order."

Municipal Education Bureau Orders All Schools to Make Up for Spring Break for One Day 106

April 7th

Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau Instruction No. 353: "It is hereby noted that Ou Yangjun, the acting principal of the Municipal First Experimental Elementary School, has reported that the spring break is scheduled for three days, from April 4th to 6th, for a total of three days. However, April 5th is Sunday and is a regular holiday. Therefore, the actual spring break is only two days. The spring scenery is beautiful and suitable for students to travel and have educational visits. The time seems to be too short. After discussions among the principals, it was agreed that it would be more convenient to give an additional day off on April 7th to make a total of three days. Please review and approve whether this is feasible. In addition to approving the additional day off on April 7th, this is hereby ordered to all municipal and registered private schools in this city. This is an order."

Xu Peihuang, Director of the Bureau
