Free Talk

One Person's Opinion 180

— Lean Sheep

▲ If I have nothing to praise and people praise me, it will only increase my shame. If I have something to praise and people praise me, it will only increase my pride.

▲ When doing things for a lover, be careful and prudent in everything, but the result may not be pleasing. When doing things for a friend, be casual, but the result may not be bad.

▲ Do not think that past events have already happened and will not be pursued, and that you are innocent. If you think about them in a quiet night, you will always feel some remorse in your conscience.

▲ The laughter of a person who is natural is everlasting, while the suffering of a person who is forced is deep.

▲ When I have not yet married, I envy the happiness of other people's couples. After I get married, I have many pains that I cannot express.

▲ It is impossible for people who have been in a dark environment for a long time to walk towards the path of light, because this kind of bad society is not easy to improve.

▲ Love is indeed sacred and inevitable for young men and women. You must know what the purpose of love is after love and how painful it will be when you lose love before you love.

▲ A person who cares about morality and integrity will never be willing to do evil, because morality and integrity are the barriers that prevent people from doing evil.

▲ When I am bored, receiving a comforting letter from a lover is like drinking nectar, but on the contrary, it is like drinking poison, which is enough to kill.

▲ No matter what the matter is, the more clues there are, the more chaotic it becomes. Borrowing a sum of money, I wish the interest would be less and lighter.

▲ Comparing fame and money, fame is indeed no match for money, but a person who cherishes fame will never be bought by money and lose his fame, because fame cannot be bought with money.

Record of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's Fund-Raising Banquet 181

— Sun Choucheng

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, in order to raise funds for the Shaanxi disaster relief, invited the President of the Control Yuan, Yu Youren, the Chairman of the National Government Relief Committee, Xu Shiying, and the Chairman of the Shaanxi Relief Committee, Kang Jiyao, to report on the disaster situation at the meeting. It specially invited all executive committee members of various industry associations to attend the lecture. Hundreds of people attended, which was an unprecedented grand occasion since the establishment of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce. The general situation has been reported in the newspapers. For the sake of pleading for the disaster victims, I will add the trivial details below to inform the philanthropists who did not attend, and ask them to generously donate to the Shaanxi Disaster Relief Association in the Renji Charity Hall on Yunnan Road so that it can be remitted to Zhu Ziqiao to personally distribute it to save the disaster victims.

▲ Crowded Signing In The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce resolved to invite the chairmen and committee members of various industry associations to be the leaders of the fundraising groups, the standing committee members to be the staff, and the executive committee members to be the members. Each group should be named after the industry it represents, and the donation amount for each group should be at least 1,000 yuan. A list of the staff members of each group was printed and distributed to the various associations. After 6:00 p.m. that evening, the committee members of various associations went to the meeting to listen to the lecture. The signing-in desk was set up at the entrance of the meeting hall. In addition to writing the name of the committee member, the name of the association must also be noted. There were too many people and too few books, so there were six or seven layers of people standing around the signing-in desk waiting to sign in, which was extremely crowded.

▲ Queuing to Enter The Room After each person signed in, they were guided by the reception staff to the standing meeting room and guest room on the third floor for tea. Because Yu Youren was concerned about disaster relief in his hometown, he arrived on time, wearing cloth socks and cloth shoes as usual. In addition to discussing disaster relief with Wang Yiting, Xu Shiying, and others, he also nodded to each industry representative as a gesture of respect. His eyebrows were still furrowed in a strong smile. It was probably because he had just returned from Shaanxi and had not forgotten the suffering of the disaster victims in his hometown. Around 7:00 p.m., because there was no space in the two rooms, Wang Xiaolai and Wu Zhihao led the guests to enter the meeting hall on the second floor. There were too many people and the door was narrow, so they entered in single file, walking in pairs like soldiers departing, which felt quite orderly.

▲ Not A Banquet The dishes that evening were provided by the Jue Lin Vegetarian Restaurant. There were five tables per row and ten rows in total, all using square tables. After seating, Wang Xiaolai stood up and stated that it was not a banquet, briefly stating that today was the 20th anniversary of the martyrdom of the seventy-two martyrs of Huanghuagang. The National Government still ordered the entire country to stop banquets on this day to express condolences. This association invited President Yu to report on the disaster situation in Shaanxi in order to raise funds for disaster relief. Because President Yu had just established the Control Yuan and his political affairs were complicated, he could not spare time except on Sundays, so he scheduled the lecture for tonight. Due to time constraints, he could not let everyone listen to the lecture on an empty stomach, so he slightly prepared some dishes, and they were all vegetarian, containing the meaning of mourning the martyrs, which did not violate the National Government's order, etc. Everyone praised his appropriate wording.

▲ Urging People To Eat First Xu Shiying said in his report, in addition to describing the process of organizing the Shanghai Temporary Emergency Relief Association for the Shaanxi Disaster and the enthusiasm of all circles, which had already donated more than 197,000 yuan, which represented the gratitude of the disaster victims, that the Shaanxi disaster film that was screened that evening was filmed by Zhu Ziqiao when he went to Shaanxi for disaster relief, recording the situations he saw at any time, including living skeletons with bones as thin as firewood, the great tragedy of entire families starving to death, those who died and had no materials to bury and howling beside them, and those who madly ate tree bark because of hunger and died on the road due to bloating. The various situations were too tragic to bear to watch. He was afraid that everyone would have difficulty swallowing after watching, so he asked them to eat well in advance before watching the film. The audience was saddened.

Record of the Scenic Spots of the Three Mountains in Zhenjiang 182

— Ma Xiezhong

My hometown, Jingkou's Three Mountains, stand in a tripod formation, and their majestic and dangerous terrain is truly an immortal scenic spot for thousands of years. According to the "Northern Gu" mountain, its name is "Northern Gu", according to the Southern History, Emperor Wu of Liang once climbed to observe it for a long time and ordered, "This ridge is not enough, it must be defended." However, Jingkou is indeed magnificent, so its name was changed from "Northern Gu". Jinshan was formed from the veins of Yinshan and its name comes from the "Flower Adornment Sutra". It has the saying that "outside Jambudvipa, in the fragrant water sea, there are seven golden mountains surrounding Mount Sumeru", and because the seawater swirls and overflows with no fixed point, seven great golden mountains are set up to stabilize it. This mountain is similar, so it is named "Jinshan". The Sanskrit word "Sumeru" in Chinese means "sublime height", so it is also named "Sublime Height Peak", also named "Golden Turtle" and "Crouching Ox", all named after their shapes, also named "Toutuo Rock" because the Tang Dynasty Pei Toutuo obtained Jin Jiao Mountain on the riverbank as the hermitage of Han Dynasty Jiao Xian, so the name "Jiao Mountain" was changed to the name "Jiao Mountain". This is how the names of the Three Mountains came about. The back peak of "Northern Gu" pillows the great river. On the upper moon, there is the Ganlu Temple. On the north cliff of the mountain, there is the Five Sages Hall. Northeast of Jinshan, there is the Chaoyang Cave. Southeast of the mountain, there is the Jinyu Rock, and the Zexin Temple is on it. West of Jiao Mountain, there is the Luohan Rock. Southwest, there is the Three Imperial Edict Cave. Its temple was formerly named Pujichan Temple. The magnificence of the palaces and temples of the Three Mountains is exhausted here. "Northern Gu" has the Shifan Building, Duojing Building, Qinghui Pavilion, Lingyun Pavilion, and Fishing Platform. Jinshan has the Miaogao Platform, Fujin Hall, Liuyu Pavilion, and Zhenliu Pavilion. Jiao Mountain has the Jiachu Pavilion, Haiyun Hall, Yinjiang Pavilion, and Yuebo Platform. "Northern Gu" has the rushing horse gully, the very stone beam, Emperor Wu of Liang's iron pot, Li Weigong's iron tower, and his hand-planted cypress trees. Jinshan has the Zhongling Spring, Su Gong's jade belt, and Zhou Ding. Jiao Mountain has the Crane Inscription Burial, the ancient tripod, the Dingtao tripod, the Han bronze drum, and the ink treasure of Yang Zhongmin Gong. There are many ancient relics, fortunately, they have not been submerged in the vicissitudes of life. Those who visit the Three Mountains, in addition to admiring the aura of the mountains and rivers, the wild grass and green smoke have not failed to make people feel emotional. Now that the spring is bright and beautiful, there are many nobles and celebrities who invite them to visit the Three Mountains. If the mountain spirits know, they will also dance with the waves.

Yue Lun Sculpture Exhibition 183

— Fang Er

The Yue Lun Sculpture Exhibition was held in the hall of the French School on Huanlong Road for ten days. On the last day, I took some time to go and see it. I recently met Yue Jun and saw his sculpture film, which had already moved my appreciation and made me want to see his real work.

Yue Jun is from my Hunan Province, the son of Yue Fushizhang (named Sen, styled Hongqun). He studied in France for eight years. In 1923, he studied painting at the National School of Fine Arts in Lyon. At the same time, he studied sculpture in the private studio of Professor Proust, a sculpture teacher at the school. Proust's studio contained many new and old masterpieces and his personal proud works. Yue Jun wandered among them, gaining extremely deep observation and understanding. After studying like this for four years, he went to Paris, the center of art, and entered the Paris National School of Fine Arts, where he studied under Bourdelle. Bourdelle was the first sculptor of modern times and was known as the first person after Rodin. The artistic feature is to emphasize the expression of strength. Yue Jun thought about doing his best. After only one year, Bourdelle passed away. Yue Jun also studied under Boerhena. Boerhe's art specializes in delicacy and is opposite to Bourdelle's sculptural expression method. Yue Jun felt a strong feeling of giving and taking the strengths of both families for his own research after being trained in a strong method and suddenly being trained in a soft method. He was greatly advanced by Boerhe. Soon after, Yue Jun rented a house outside of Paris, leaving the teacher to study alone. From the winter of 1928 to the spring of 1930, he created many works. First, he participated in the Lyon Art Research Association's exhibition in 1929 and won an honorary certificate. Then, he went to the French Artists Federation's 1930 Paris Salon exhibition and won the highest honorary certificate and received great praise in the Paris newspapers.

This exhibition back in China brings back a dozen or so pieces that can be brought back. I looked at his works, and in terms of strength, I loved his "Old Man" and "Human Body", and in terms of softness, I loved his "Self-Portrait" and "Portrait of Ms. R" "Portrait of My Wife", as well as "Sun Yat-sen's Portrait", "Liao Zhongkai's Portrait", and "Tan Zu'an's Portrait" are all lifelike and exquisite.

His exhibition has inscriptions by contemporary celebrities, and I love Mr. Yi Peiji's inscription "Its Art is Brilliant" the most. The word is very unique, and the inscription "White House Residence" is even more unique.

Talk About Wolfberry 184

— Qingqu

Wolfberry is the only vegetable dish that is usually eaten in my county recently. It is said that the spring air is warm and the shoots germinate and develop here, which is very prosperous. When people in the countryside carry vegetables into the market, almost no one does not have them, and the profits are also higher. In the beginning, the price was extremely expensive, and every two taels of copper coins had to be ten pieces to get their permission, so old gluttons would not hesitate to buy them to taste their taste, and those who struggled to make a living would not dare to ask about them even if they saw them.

This thing does not grow in the wilderness, but always on the side of the fence or on the wall slope, so it cannot be planted and picked. It is also not easy to find at first. There is not much production in the county, and most of it is transshipped from Taicang. Because the people of Lou eat very little, it can be used to supplement here and the price can gradually flatten. At present, it is almost everywhere in the market, which also shows that one side has a special addiction. Looking at its cooking method, it is also different from other places. Wolfberry tastes bitter and astringent, so even the best chefs must add heavy sugar to make it palatable, or even fry it in lard, just like the Shanghai Sichuan and Fujian restaurants. I don't know that it is too thick and greasy, so it loses its original nature. Therefore, my county is just stir-fried, even fragrant mushrooms and sesame oil are not allowed to be added a little, only enough vegetable oil is enough. What cannot be missing is not bamboo shoots, and its taste is not beautiful. The most taboo is soy sauce, if you violate it, it will lose its sweetness and forget its inherent quality. Those who don't know how to eat this thing are not good at eating wolfberry. The records about wolfberry are not the same. It is a shrub and Lanya says, "Eating its roots can lighten the body and benefit the qi", which is called the holy medicine, probably referring to the wolfberry root bark. The Ben Cao has a saying that "it can be used as a fairy's staff", which is to describe its old branches and bent shape. Or it is called "Heavenly Essence Son", and its red seeds can also be used as medicine, but it does not say that eating its fat and tender branches and leaves shows that eating this has not started since ancient times, but it has become popular in modern times. However, customs vary from place to place, and hobbies are also different. I don't know why there are so many people who like to eat it in my county alone, so I specifically describe it.

▲ News from the Publishing World Yang Yunshi is talented and has the eyes of a contemporary talent. His poems are as good as the Tang sages, and his five-character poems are almost unmatched in the world. I have seen his Tianshan Song Seven Ancient poems, which reached more than 2,600 words. Recently, I saw another article, Vomiting Blood Chant Five Ancient poems, which reached 240 rhymes. His seven-character poems are amazing and his five-character poems are like Du Fu resurrected. I heard that his complete works will be sold by the Zhenmei Shan Bookstore in the near future, printed by the Zhonghua Bookstore in Song edition style, with exquisite craftsmanship. It is expected that once this collection comes out, Luoyang will be short of paper. Last year, Fan Fanshan died in error, and the literati were shocked and told each other that from then on, the leader would be none other than Yunshi. Now that Fanshan is dead, and Yunshi's poetry collection has been published, I know that once this collection comes out, the poetry genre in the country will definitely change. This is also a major key to the change in modern poetry (Chunmu)

India Travelogue (11) 185

— Linghua

On the 30th, a monk brought a letter of introduction from University Professor D. P. Bagchi. The monk's name was Satyawanda. Professor Bagchi was introducing a Chinese scholar, the monk Satyawanda, who wished to organize the Asiatic League of Culture. Professor Bagchi had traveled to China and written the book Deux Lexiquues Sanskrit_Chinois Tome i, also named "News of Sanskrit and Tang Dynasties," as well as the Thousand Character Classic, and the “Meaning of Cleanliness” and “Miscellaneous Names in Sanskrit” collected by the Kucha Śramaṇa Liyan in a Japanese edition with phonetic annotations by Professor Bagchi. It is an essential book for learning Sanskrit. The monk Satyawanda showed me the charter of his Asiatic League of Culture. I originally intended to discuss it with the charter of the Oriental Literary Renaissance Society. The monk had studied Marxist theory. Observing Marxism from an Indian perspective, he was naturally dissatisfied. Therefore, he wanted to correct the flaws of Western materialism with Eastern art, literature, and philosophy. I advised him to travel to China and Japan to connect and advance together.

In the afternoon, I went with an Indian friend to the Bengli Botanic Garden. From the corner of the university, we took a tram to Strand Road High Court. Each person paid two annas and got off to wait for a small ferry. This is the bank of the sacred Ganges. The Ganges originates in Tibet, gathers water from various places, flows to Calcutta, and enters the Bay of Bengal at its mouth. The water is not very clear, resembling the Yellow River, but it is calm and without waves at its entrance, which is not very wide, only about the size of our Zhun'er Bao Mi Ke said that the Ganges was an ancient holy land, rumored to originate in heaven. According to the Tibetan Plateau, its source is from heaven. This agrees with Li Bai's poem, "The Yellow River's water comes from heaven," but it has been falsely spread into mythology. Many people bathe in the Ganges, including women, all wearing clothes. Having come to this holy land, I could not but receive a baptism. After crossing to the north bank near the botanical garden, I chose a place to wash my head and feet. Indeed, my body and mind felt cleansed. The greatest memory of the Ganges for us is that people in China have almost all seen the Surangama Sutra. The sutra contains a dialogue between the Buddha and King Pasenadi, roughly saying, "Your Majesty, when did you see the Ganges?" The king said, "When I was three years old, my loving mother took me to visit Jivaka. At that time, I knew there was the Ganges." Such stories are not only philosophical cases but also evoke boundless deep feelings of gratitude and filial piety. We waited half an hour in the waiting room for the small ferry to come. Tickets were bought for four annas per person for first class and two annas for second class. After getting on the boat, we stopped twice, the second time at the botanical garden. Indian guards in red turbans with long poles guarded the gate. No fee was required to enter. The trees were so tall that they reached into the clouds, with little sunlight reaching here. It was a truly cool and refreshing place. I originally had a deeper interest in studying plants. I once translated the complete volume of "Great Botany" by Japanese scholar Miyoshi Manabu with Mr. Sun Jianhong. However, I cannot now record many plant names. The garden is large, more than a square mile. Many people visit it, and Western ladies also come to visit on Sundays. There are also small signs indicating the scientific names of the plants, but not many, which is a pity. What is memorable is the banyan tree, which is 157 years old, 890 feet high, and has a circumference occupying 1,000 feet. The aerial roots extend and grow, forming another tree, with almost half an acre of land. It has become a pavilion where houses can be built. It is a remarkable sight. I have written a poem to record it:

The botanical garden borders the Ganges to the north,

Myriad trees reach the clouds, obscuring the sky.

Most beloved are the banyan mother and child trees,

Whose spreading roots have stood for a hundred and ten years.

Financial Gold Rush Surge 186

High Jump and Weak Nian

Unexpectedly Rising Step by Step Yesterday, the gold price on April 1st started weakly, then gradually became highly sought after. The upward momentum was unstoppable. The market moved progressively higher. There were only two or three taels of variation. The total difference in the market was 23 taels. In the end, it surged by 20 taels. The exchange rate trend was smooth, and the listed price was reduced by one grade. The market's demand exceeded supply. There were no changes in the overseas silver market, so the gold price opened low. Afterwards, Hengxing vigorously covered short positions, and major players rushed to buy, pushing the exchange rate even higher. People were shocked, and the price soared, surging by 20 taels. The market still felt strong, and buyers remained active, pushing the price beyond 720 taels. The final price was 724.5 taels. The speed of the rise was truly unexpected. In short, the Guang bang's covering of short positions was stimulated by the fact that the foreign exchange market was closed on Wednesday afternoon. The prediction for this morning was that the price would fall.

The opening was still weak. The May opening in the morning fell slightly by 2.5 mace, reaching 702.5 taels. This was because the prediction was bearish, so there was no movement. After the market closed, there were considerable purchases from the United States, but the private telegram only reported a decrease of 125. As a result, confidence seemed to weaken, with a rise and fall of one or two taels, from 04 taels falling to 02 taels. Then Hengxing and others sold, and suddenly it rose again to 04 taels because Maccari bought one unit of April British gold at 1375. The Dalian bang settled on 1.5 mace and 5 fen for each unit of current-month Dalian gold. Subsequently, Huabi and others released 75 units of current-month British gold, so the gold price was suppressed again to 02.5 taels. The first order was issued not to change, and it was 03.23 mace. However, the internal price seemed firm at 1375. Then the Macao bank released 6875, and the price rose to 06 taels. Before long, it depreciated by 2 taels to 04 taels. At 10:00, because Hengxing Shengda, Hengxing Yuan, Cuichang Xiangyi, and others fought to buy, the peak was reached, and the price soared into the sky, rising more than 10 taels. At 10:50, it had exceeded 710 taels, moving very quickly, with only a little more than one tael. Then, the price continued to advance. At 10:50, the Fung exchange suddenly reduced the grade by half, with British gold calculated at 125, US dollars at 25, and Japanese gold increased by 1.25 fen, so the price rose to 717.8 taels. Hengxing and others continued to drag in, reaching 20 taels at 11:00. Soon, retail investors and speculators sold, falling by more than 3 taels to 16.5 taels. Afterwards, the exchange market was even tighter. May and June British gold only settled at 13.5 to 4375. Then Xinxing and others chased to buy, so it broke through the 20-tael mark again. At 11:45, the British gold continued to reduce the grade by half, with 125 for British gold, 25 for US dollars, and 1.25 fen for Japanese gold. The price immediately rose to 23.5 taels. At this time, there seemed to be more sellers, and many short-term holders also sold, so it fell sharply by 4 taels to 19.5 taels. However, confidence remained high, and the price was pushed up to 22 taels. At noon, the listed price was changed to 771.478 to 50 taels.

Strong upward surge in the afternoon. The market opened flat in the afternoon at 21 taels, then decreased to 19 taels. Afterwards, there was a fluctuation of one or two taels. Only when the Indian exchange rate reported a small increase of two annas did the buyers become active at 2:30, rising to 22 taels. However, because the exchange market was closed on Wednesday, it retreated to 20.05 taels around 3:00. Afterwards, Yuan Mao, Yong Yu, Da Qian, Chang Xiang, and others bought, so the price rose by more than 3 taels to 23.9 taels at 3:30. In a flash, it fell by more than 3 taels to 20.05 taels, probably due to the Dalian gang and others selling. Subsequently, Chengfeng, Yong Yuan, Mao Yong, Changsheng Yong, and others bought one after another, raising the price by more than 4 taels in just over 10 minutes, reaching 25 taels at 3:50. After 4:00, it was slightly suppressed by a little more than one tael. At 4:30, the market closed at 24.8 taels as Yuancheng and others took delivery. Compared to the previous day, it rose by 19.8 taels. Hengxing came to sell the whole day. The maximum price was 25 taels, and the minimum price was 02 taels, with a total difference of 23 taels. Looking back at the morning market, the goods were priced at 2 taels and 3 mace. The noon closing was 21 taels. The afternoon closed at 21 taels, and the listed price was 50 to 467 taels. The registered price was 17 to 21 taels, and the water compensation was 17 taels. The afternoon price was 21 taels.

A glimpse of buyers' activities. Transactions were quite active at various firms. Qian Changxiang, Cuichang Yong, Chengfeng Yong, Yuan Tai, Xinxing, and Zhifeng Yong all advanced. Hengxing Yuan and a certain Mr. Lu also advanced, becoming bullish. Fuchang and Yuanheng advanced and then exited. Shunli, Wanxing, Dadecheng, Changsheng Yong, Yuhe, and others came and went. Tong Taichang, Yuancheng, Futaiheng, and Yuan Mao Yong also exited. Hengxing and Shengda sold slightly at first and then vigorously covered short positions by a huge amount of 10,000 units. Youth Zone

Results of the Essay Competition of the Guangming Society of the College of Political Science and Law 203

--- Text

The fashion of academic research is indeed an indispensable factor for us today. We acknowledge that under the modern education system, relying solely on books or lectures can by no means satisfy our thirst for knowledge. We must seek other ways to develop and avoid the pain of suffocation. Therefore, extracurricular activities are indeed a quality we eagerly need. There, we can explore a new expression of life that cannot be obtained in the bustling classroom. Therefore, the general urgency of young students in organizing academic groups within or outside the school should be consciously pursued after realizing this point. Although, if we put in some effort to analyze it in detail, it would not be so simple, but the superficial exposure is mostly like this. The Guangming Society of the College of Political Science and Law is a product of this. It is an outstanding one among the academic groups in the College of Political Science and Law. I remember having introduced it here before. Their concerted efforts in their work are indeed worthy of admiration. Since the beginning of this semester, although the work has been interrupted for some time due to certain reasons, recently it has revived its inherent spirit and reorganized its affairs. A fundraising committee has been resolved in the executive committee to raise funds from inside and outside the school to subsidize the shortage of funds, which is now underway. The second is to organize a spring break travel group, wanting to throw themselves into the arms of West Lake in the great spring light and indulge for a while. Another important thing is to plan to publish a yearbook as a memorial, with the carefully crafted works of the members published, with about 100,000 words. It has been handed over to Zhu Airen and Li Chunsen of the publishing department to plan everything. If it can be realized, it will be very meaningful, and the expression of this kind of work is also closely related to the reputation of the school. The essay competition was set up by the society to increase interest. The topic was "Youth and Politics." Students inside and outside the society enthusiastically submitted articles, and a total of 57 essays were received. Originally, there were prizes for the top three, but now because there are so many good works, it is unbearable to go against the general elegance, so the prize amount was temporarily expanded by three. After evaluation, the results were: first place, Zhu Jianbai, prize: a silver shield with the inscription "Substance in Words"; second place, Li Ming, prize: a silver frame with the inscription "Containing Essence and Chewing Flowers"; third place, Lu Chaofan, prize: a silk banner with the inscription "Brush Sweeps a Thousand Armies"; fourth place, Meng Berlin; fifth place, Shun; sixth place, Wang Shiying, each prize: a "Vanguard Monthly." This move is a pioneering one among the academic groups in the College of Political Science and Law.

To West Lake 204

— Su Jun

Extreme neurasthenia made me begin to get tired of the city. Squeezed in a crowded streetcar, my head was dizzy, my chest could not breathe, and my heart felt like vomiting.

—Go to West Lake and stay for a while. I was sick, really sick. In the vibration of the streetcar, I thought to myself. Back in the house, I told Hai and Zou. They were shocked. "Fun!" Zou jumped up and said, "Suddenly thinking of going to West Lake again. West Lake is still very lonely at this time."

"You," Hai said, "you admirer of the city, you are going to admire nature again?"

"I'm sick," I replied to them, "because I've been too far away from nature. I want to be soothed in the embrace of nature. I want to escape the noise. Loneliness is useful to me."

"Then you really decided to go?" they asked.

"Yes," I replied, "and I'm going tomorrow."

They were silent with shock.

In the morning, Hai put me on the bus.

"Hey," Hai said to me, "You go. If you say West Lake is better to live in than Shanghai, I will come too."

"But," I said, "West Lake is too poetic. I don't want to live there for a long time. I just want to clear my mind and let the fresher air soothe me. I will still come back. I can't leave the city because I can't leave the real life of the world."

The bus was about to leave. Hai went down for a while and then came back to give me a bunch of bananas and a newspaper. Then the bus wriggled. I shook Hai's hand. "Goodbye, Hai." Goodbye, Shanghai.

After five hours of driving, the bus arrived at the train station.

After unloading my luggage at a hotel, I went to see West Lake. Ah, West Lake is already in spring. The willows on Su Causeway are green, and the tourists in the lakeside park are wearing thin jackets...

Passing through Bai Causeway, passing the gate of the National Art College, there was the sound of piano jumping out from the wall. Young female students were walking. They are worthy of pride. I quickly walked past them so they wouldn't know I was there. I found Mr. Xu in Yu Lou.

"Ah," Mr. Xu exclaimed strangely, "how did you come?"

I was very ashamed and uneasy. A year ago, I had argued with Mr. Xu over a small matter that people wouldn't believe. Now I've run to him again. I don't know if he still remembers those past events.

With Mr. Xu and the others, after passing Inner West Lake and Yue Fei's tomb, we found a small house at the foot of Qixia Ridge. It was next to a ancestral hall, near the cemetery. The environment was quiet and solemn, but close to West Lake. Through the bars of the iron gate, we could see the flowing water of West Lake, calm and clear, like lively eyes.

Youth Zone Guidelines 205

(1) Articles should be about discussions on youth issues, news about domestic and foreign studies or students, essays, descriptions of school life, random notes, etc. The style is not limited.

(2) Books are limited to those concerning youth issues.

(3) Photos that qualify are those related to youth life (such as sports, travel, tours, drama performances, speeches, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movements. Both individual and group photos are welcome.

(4) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(5) The number of words in each article should not exceed 2,000.

(6) Do not write manuscripts horizontally. Do not write sloppily. Save Western text where possible. If it is unavoidable to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.
